(pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go):**\\nThe `Signature` struct implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface and is responsible for reading and verifying plugin manifests. Key methods include:\\n- `Calculate()`: Calculates the plugin's signature state by reading the manifest and verifying file hashes\\n- `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()`: Reads the MANIFEST.txt file containing the plugin signature\\n- `readPluginManifest()`: Decodes and parses the PGP-signed manifest\\n- `validateManifest()`: Validates required manifest fields and verifies the PGP signature\\n- `Verify()`: Performs PGP signature verification using OpenPGP libraries\\n\\nThe manifest structure (PluginManifest) contains plugin ID, version, signature type, signing organization, file hashes, and root URLs for private/community plugins.\\n\\n**Signature Validation on Load (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go):**\\nThe `Validation` struct implements the `Validator` interface and handles signature validation at load time:\\n- `ValidateSignature()`: Validates plugin signatures and handles signature inheritance for child plugins\\n- Uses a `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` to check if unsigned plugins are allowed\\n- Returns appropriate plugin errors for invalid, modified, or unsigned plugins\\n\\n**Unsigned Plugin Allowlist Enforcement (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go):**\\nThe `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` implements the `PluginLoaderAuthorizer` interface:\\n- `CanLoadPlugin()`: Determines if an unsigned plugin can be loaded by checking:\\n  1. Dev mode status (allows unsigned plugins in development)\\n  2. Plugin ID against the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n  3. Returns true only if the plugin is in the allowlist or dev mode is enabled\\n\\n## Public Key Retrieval System\\n\\n**Static Key Retriever (pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go):**\\nProvides a hardcoded Grafana public key for signature verification:\\n- `GetPublicKey()`: Returns the static PGP public key for a given key ID\\n- Falls back to this when dynamic key retrieval is disabled\\n\\n**Dynamic Key Retriever (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go):**\\nManages dynamic retrieval and caching of public keys from grafana.com API:\\n- `GetPublicKey()`: Retrieves public keys from cache (kv storage)\\n- `downloadKeys()`: Fetches plugin signing keys from the grafana.com API endpoint\\n- Implements automatic key syncing every 10 days with cache validation\\n- `ensureKeys()`: Initializes key storage with the default static key if empty\\n\\n**Key Retriever Service (pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/retriever.go):**\\nAggregates static and dynamic key retrieval:\\n- `GetPublicKey()`: Routes to dynamic key retriever if enabled, otherwise uses static key\\n\\n## Validation Pipeline Integration\\n\\n**Validation Pipeline (pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go):**\\nImplements the signature validation step in the plugin loading pipeline:\\n- `SignatureValidationStep()`: Creates a ValidateFunc for signature validation\\n- Integrates with the validation pipeline to check signatures before plugin initialization\\n\\n**Bootstrap Stage (pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go):**\\nCalculates signatures during the bootstrap phase:\\n- `DefaultConstructor.Construct()`: Uses SignatureCalculator to calculate plugin signatures\\n- Integrates manifest signing verification into the plugin construction process\\n\\n## Configuration and Settings\\n\\n**Plugin Configuration (pkg/plugins/config/config.go):**\\nDefines checking\\n\\n**Settings Reader (pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go):**\\nReads plugin configuration from the Grafana config file:\\n- Reads `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting from the [plugins] section\\n- Also reads key retrieval settings: `public_key_retrieval_disabled`, `public_key_retrieval_on_startup`\\n\\n## Core Interfaces\\n\\n**Key Interfaces (pkg/plugins/ifaces.go):**\\n- calculator into the bootstrap stage\\n- Integrates signature validator into the validation stage\\n- Wires together all components in the plugin loading pipeline\\n\\n**Wire Bindings (pkg/plugins/models.go):**\\n- SignatureStatusValid: Signed and verified\\n- SignatureStatusInvalid: Invalid signature\\n- SignatureStatusModified: Valid signature but file contents modified\\n- SignatureStatusUnsigned: No MANIFEST.txt file\\n- SignatureStatusInternal: Core plugin with no signature\\n\\n## Signature Verification Flow\\n\\nThe complete flow is:\\n1. OpenPGP signature verification confirms the manifest wasn't tampered with\\n6. File hashes in the manifest are verified against actual plugin files\\n7.
